## Финальный документ Part VI

```python
"""
Part VI Final Report
====================
Monostring Fragmentation: Summary of findings

This script generates the definitive summary figure
for Part VI, documenting what was confirmed,
what was falsified, and what was newly discovered.
"""

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import matplotlib.gridspec as gridspec
from matplotlib.patches import FancyArrowPatch
import matplotlib.patches as mpatches

# Data from v7-v11 (hardcoded confirmed results)
# These are means over multiple runs

# Finding 1: D_corr of different orbits
dcorr_data = {
    'E6\n(Coxeter)':    (3.013, 0.125),
    'Shuf E6\n(same ω)': (3.057, 0.159),
    'Rand\n(uniform)':  (5.542, 0.072),
}

# Finding 2: ΔS profile (v11, n=30)
dS_profile = {
    20:  (+0.0003, 0.9944),
    30:  (-0.1741, 0.0000),
    40:  (-0.2387, 0.0000),
    60:  (-0.0294, 0.3694),
    80:  (-0.0173, 0.6257),
    120: (+0.1190, 0.0005),
    170: (-0.0230, 0.4376),
    250: (+0.0136, 0.6986),
    350: (+0.0744, 0.0481),
    500: (+0.0238, 0.3904),
    700: (-0.1499, 0.0000),
    1000:(-0.0753, 0.0113),
}

# Finding 3: τ(σ)
tau_sigma = {
    0.20: 228.0,
    0.35: 236.4,
    0.50: 236.9,
    0.70: 235.4,
    1.00: 237.1,
}

# Finding 4: τ by frequency type
tau_freqs = {
    'E6':         297.1,
    'Shuf E6':    321.0,
    'Arithmetic': 100.4,
    'Uniform':    None,
    'Geometric':  None,
}

fig = plt.figure(figsize=(24, 18))
fig.patch.set_facecolor('#f8f9fa')
fig.suptitle(
    "Monostring Hypothesis — Part VI: Fragmentation\n"
    "Summary of 11 computational experiments",
    fontsize=16, fontweight='bold', y=0.99,
    color='#1a1a2e')

gs = gridspec.GridSpec(
    3, 4, figure=fig,
    hspace=0.50, wspace=0.40)


# ── Panel 1: D_corr of orbits ─────────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[0, 0])
ax.set_facecolor('#f0f4f8')

labels = list(dcorr_data.keys())
means  = [dcorr_data[k][0] for k in labels]
stds   = [dcorr_data[k][1] for k in labels]
colors = ['#2196F3', '#FF9800', '#4CAF50']

bars = ax.bar(range(len(labels)), means,
               yerr=stds, capsize=8,
               color=colors, alpha=0.85,
               edgecolor='k', linewidth=1.2,
               error_kw=dict(elinewidth=2))

ax.axhline(3.02, c='red', ls='--', lw=2,
           label='Part V: 3.02', zorder=5)
ax.fill_between([-0.5, 2.5], [2.7, 2.7],
                [3.35, 3.35], alpha=0.08,
                color='red', label='±0.35 band')

ax.set_xticks(range(len(labels)))
ax.set_xticklabels(labels, fontsize=9)
ax.set_ylabel('D_corr', fontsize=11)
ax.set_title('Finding 1: D_corr of orbits\n'
             'E6 ≈ Shuf ≈ 3.02  ≠  Rand',
             fontsize=10, fontweight='bold')
ax.legend(fontsize=8)
ax.set_ylim([0, 7])
ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')

# Annotate
ax.annotate('Same!', xy=(0.5, 3.2),
            fontsize=11, ha='center',
            color='darkblue', fontweight='bold')
ax.annotate('Different!', xy=(2, 5.8),
            fontsize=11, ha='center',
            color='darkgreen', fontweight='bold')


# ── Panel 2: ΔS(t) profile ────────────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[0, 1:3])
ax.set_facecolor('#f0f4f8')

T_arr  = sorted(dS_profile.keys())
dS_arr = [dS_profile[t][0] for t in T_arr]
pv_arr = [dS_profile[t][1] for t in T_arr]

# Color regions
for i in range(len(T_arr)-1):
    t1, t2 = T_arr[i], T_arr[i+1]
    d1, d2 = dS_arr[i], dS_arr[i+1]
    mid_d  = (d1+d2)/2
    c      = '#c8e6c9' if mid_d < 0 else '#ffcdd2'
    ax.fill_between([t1,t2], [d1,d2], 0,
                    alpha=0.4, color=c)

ax.plot(T_arr, dS_arr, 'o-',
        c='#1565C0', lw=2.5, ms=8,
        zorder=4, label='ΔS(t)')
ax.axhline(0, c='k', lw=2, zorder=3)

# Mark significant points
for t, d, p in zip(T_arr, dS_arr, pv_arr):
    if p < 0.01 and d < 0:
        ax.scatter(t, d, s=150, c='#2E7D32',
                   zorder=6, edgecolors='k',
                   linewidth=1.5)
    elif p < 0.01:
        ax.scatter(t, d, s=150, c='#C62828',
                   zorder=6, edgecolors='k',
                   linewidth=1.5)
    elif p < 0.05:
        ax.scatter(t, d, s=100, c='#F57F17',
                   zorder=6, edgecolors='k',
                   linewidth=1)

# Annotations
ax.annotate('E6 more\nordered',
            xy=(35, -0.23), fontsize=10,
            color='#2E7D32', ha='center',
            fontweight='bold')
ax.annotate('(oscillates)', xy=(200, 0.08),
            fontsize=9, color='gray',
            ha='center', style='italic')
ax.annotate('E6 more\nordered again',
            xy=(700, -0.15), fontsize=10,
            color='#2E7D32', ha='center',
            fontweight='bold')

ax.set_xlabel('t (evolution steps)', fontsize=11)
ax.set_ylabel('ΔS = S(E6) − S(Shuf)', fontsize=11)
ax.set_title(
    'Finding 2: Entropy difference ΔS(t)\n'
    '● green=E6 ordered (p<0.01)  '
    '● red=Shuf ordered (p<0.01)  '
    '● orange=p<0.05',
    fontsize=10, fontweight='bold')
ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)


# ── Panel 3: τ(σ) ─────────────────────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[0, 3])
ax.set_facecolor('#f0f4f8')

sigmas = sorted(tau_sigma.keys())

ax.plot(sigmas, taus, 'o-', c='#1565C0',
        lw=2.5, ms=12,
        markerfacecolor='white',
        markeredgewidth=2.5)

           ls='--', lw=1.5,
           label=f'mean={np.mean(taus[1:]):.0f}')

ax.set_xlabel('σ (fragmentation width)', fontsize=11)
ax.set_ylabel('τ_E6 (crossover steps)', fontsize=11)
ax.set_title('Finding 3: τ vs σ\n'
             'τ ≈ const (σ-independent!)',
             fontsize=10, fontweight='bold')
ax.legend(fontsize=9)
ax.set_ylim([0, 450])
ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)

ax.annotate('τ ≈ 236 steps\n(σ-independent)',
            xy=(0.60, 236), xytext=(0.65, 320),
            fontsize=9, color='red',
            arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->',
                            color='red'))


# ── Panel 4: τ by frequency type ──────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[1, 0])
ax.set_facecolor('#f0f4f8')

freq_names = ['E6', 'Shuf\nE6',
              'Arith-\nmetic', 'Uniform',
              'Geo-\nmetric']
freq_taus  = [297.1, 321.0, 100.4, 0, 0]
freq_colors= ['#2196F3', '#FF9800',
               '#9C27B0', '#9E9E9E', '#9E9E9E']

               color=freq_colors, alpha=0.85,
               edgecolor='k', linewidth=1)

             'Irrationality → longer τ',
             fontsize=10, fontweight='bold')
ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')

# Label bars
for bar, val in zip(bars2, freq_taus):
    if val > 0:
        ax.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2,
                val + 5, f'{val:.0f}',
                ha='center', va='bottom',
                fontsize=9, fontweight='bold')
    else:
        ax.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2,
                15, 'N/A',
                ha='center', va='bottom',
                fontsize=9, color='gray')


# ── Panel 5: Falsified claims ─────────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[1, 1])

        transform=ax.transAxes,

# ── Panel 6: Confirmed claims ─────────────────────────
ax = fig.add_subplot(gs[1, 2])
ax.set_facecolor('#e8f5e9')
ax.axis('off')

confirmed = [
```

## Итоговый вывод Part VI

```
Гипотеза фрагментации моноструны в её
исходной формулировке ОПРОВЕРГНУТА:

❌ Дочерние струны не сходятся к орбите
❌ E6 не уникальна (Shuffled даёт то же)
❌ Нет монотонной стрелы времени

НО обнаружены три реальных эффекта:

✅ D_corr(orbit) = 3.02 — устойчивый результат
   Определяется набором частот, не порядком

✅ ΔS(t=30-40) < 0 (p<0.0001)
   Начальный порядок от общего происхождения

✅ τ ≈ 237 шагов, σ-независимое
   Возможно τ ∝ h(E6) = 12 (Coxeter number)

Следующий шаг: проверить τ ∝ h для
других алгебр (E7: h=18, E8: h=30, A6: h=7)
Это было бы первым доказательством того,
что E6 структура ВЛИЯЕТ на динамику фрагментации.
```
